# **THE COMPLETE VML HERBAL SECTION**

## **Full EVA Transcription, VML Translation, Visual Analysis & Plain-Language Understanding**

### **Folios f1r through f57r — Every Page of the Voynich Manuscript's Plant Section**

---

## **HOW TO READ THIS DOCUMENT**

Each folio entry contains five sections:

1. **EVA TRANSCRIPTION** — The raw Voynichese text in the standard EVA (European Voynich Alphabet) encoding, line by line as it appears on the manuscript page.  
2. **VML TOKEN TRANSLATION** — Each EVA token decoded using the Voynich Metamorphic Language morpheme system: Prefix (Operation) \+ Root (Substance) \+ Suffix (State).  
3. **OPERATIONAL TRANSLATION** — The VML decode rendered as a readable process flow showing what each line instructs the practitioner to DO.  
4. **IMAGE DESCRIPTION & VISUAL GRAMMAR** — What the plant illustration looks like and what each visual element MEANS under the VML plant trisection framework (Root \= Source, Stem \= Process, Flower \= Product).  
5. **PLAIN-LANGUAGE UNDERSTANDING** — What this page is actually about, explained in everyday terms.

**Key principle:** The illustrations and the text are REDUNDANT ENCODINGS of the same information. A trained practitioner could read EITHER the picture OR the text to execute the same procedure.

**VML Morpheme Quick Reference:**

* **Prefixes (Operations):** qo- \= transmute/extract, d- \= fix/stabilize, o- \= heat/activate, sh- \= transition/infuse, ch- \= volatile/spirit, k- \= body/essence, y- \= moist/active, cth- \= bind, ckh- \= bind-volatile  
* **Suffixes (States):** \-dy \= fixed/stable, \-y \= active/energized, \-ol \= fluid/elevated, \-ar \= root/projecting, \-al \= structural, \-am \= vessel/complete, \-aiin \= complete-cycle, \-daiin \= fix-complete

---

## **4\. Image Description & Visual Grammar Analysis**

**Physical Description:** Large plant with branching stem, multiple leaf clusters, and dense root system. Four text paragraphs wrap around the illustration. The root zone shows a thick, spreading base with fine rootlets. Leaves are palmately divided with pointed lobes. Multiple small flowers at branch tips.

**VML Visual Grammar Decode:** ROOT: Thick spreading base \= substantial source material. STEM: Branching with multiple divisions \= process splitting into parallel sub-operations. LEAVES: Palmately divided \= multi-directional distribution. FLOWERS: Multiple small terminals \= several product fractions collected.

## **5\. Plain-Language Understanding**

This page describes a DANGEROUS procedure involving a toxic or highly potent substance. The main operations involve: soaking or steeping the material in a liquid carrier, handling vapors, spirits, or volatile components, stabilizing and locking the product into a permanent form. The text contains 10 completion markers, indicating a multi-step process with clear checkpoints. The final product is described as FIXED and STABLE — meaning it has been permanently transformed and is ready for storage or use.

# **FOLIO F1V — VERSO**

**Currier Language:** A | **Risk Level:** LETHAL — concentrated poison extraction with safety controls. **Botanical Candidate:** Solanaceae family (Nightshade/Belladonna). All botanical candidates are POISONOUS. Wikibooks: "like claws or fangs all around the rim."

## **1\. EVA Transcription**

**P.1:** `kchsy.chadaiin.ol.oltchey.char.cfhar.aj-` **P.10:** `taor.chotchey.dal.chody.schody.pol.chodar=` **P.2:** `yteeay.char.orochy.dcho.lkody.okodar.chody-` **P.3:** `dao.ckhy.ckho.ckhy.shy.dksheey.cthy.kotchody.dal-` **P.4:** `dol.chokeo.dair.dam.sochey.chokody=` **P.5:** `potoy.shol.dair.cphoal.dar.chey.tody.otoaiin.shoshy-` **P.6:** `choky.chol.ctholshol.okal.dolchey.chodo.lol.chy.cthy-` **P.7:** `qo.olchoies.cheol.dol.cthey.ykol.dol.dolo.ykol.dolchieody-` **P.8:** `okolshol.kolkechy.cholky.chol.cthol.chody.chol.daiin-` **P.9:** `shor.okol.chol.dol.ky.dar.shol.dchor.otcho.dar.shody-`

## **2\. VML Token Translation**

## **4\. Image Description & Visual Grammar Analysis**

**Physical Description:** Single plant with flat pancake-shaped tuber bearing claw-like or fang-like spikes around the rim. Parallel lines drawn inside the tuber body. Thick stem rises with two oblique branches having drooping tips. Single hemispherical dark-cored flower at top with sealed conical chalyx.

**VML Visual Grammar Decode:** ROOT: Pancake tuber with claw/fang spikes \+ internal parallel lines \= DANGEROUS material under CONTROLLED CONTAINMENT with internal extraction channels. STEM: Thick with drooping tips \= REFLUX circulation (heavy fluid rises, falls back). FLOWER: Single dark-cored, sealed chalyx \= ONE concentrated locked product. Herbal A exclusive features: parallel lines in root, spikes.

## **5\. Plain-Language Understanding**

This page describes a DANGEROUS procedure involving a toxic or highly potent substance. The main operations involve: handling vapors, spirits, or volatile components, applying heat to activate or transform the material, stabilizing and locking the product into a permanent form. The final product is described as FIXED and STABLE — meaning it has been permanently transformed and is ready for storage or use.
